// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // 10 time units period
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;

        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle the T flip-flop to the "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0; // Keep it stable to observe the state

        // Finish the simulation
        #20 $finish;
    end

endmodule
Compilation check...

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // 10 time units period
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;

        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle the T flip-flop to "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0;

        // End simulation after some time
        #50 $finish;
    end

endmodule

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // Toggle clock every 5 time units
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;
        
        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1; // Activate reset
        #10 reset = 0; // Deactivate reset

        // Toggle T flip-flop to "1" state
        #10 t = 1; // Set T to 1 to toggle the state
        #10 t = 0; // Set T to 0 to hold the state

        // Finish simulation
        #50 $finish;
    end

endmodule

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

        .reset(reset),

        .q(q)

    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // 10 time units period
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;

        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle the T flip-flop to the "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0; // Keep it stable to observe the state

        // Finish the simulation
        #20 $finish;
    end

    // Monitor outputs
    initial begin
        $monitor("At time %t: clk = %b, reset = %b, t = %b, q = %b", $time, clk, reset, t, q);
    end

endmodule
Compilation check...

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // 10 time units period
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;

        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle the T flip-flop to the "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0; // Keep it stable to observe the state

        // Finish the simulation
        #50 $finish;
    end

    // Monitor outputs

    end

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // 10 time units period
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;

        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle the T flip-flop to "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0;

        // End simulation after some time
        #50 $finish;
    end

endmodule

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // Toggle clock every 5 time units
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;
        
        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle T to set the flip-flop to "1"
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0; // Toggling back to 0 to hold the state

        // Finish simulation
        #50 $finish;
    end

endmodule

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop

        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // Toggle clock every 5 time units
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;
        
        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;
        
        // Toggle to "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0; // Maintain state
        #10 t = 1; // Toggle back
        #10 t = 0; // Maintain state
        
        // Finish simulation
        #20 $finish;
    end

endmodule

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // 10 time units period
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;

        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle the T flip-flop to "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0;

        // End simulation after some time
        #50 $finish;
    end

endmodule
Compilation check...

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // 10 time units period
    end

    // Testbench
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;

        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle the T flip-flop to "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0;

        // End simulation after some time
        #50 $finish;
    end

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // 10 time units period
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;

        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle the T flip-flop to "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0;

        // End simulation after some time
        #50 $finish;
    end

endmodule

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // Toggle clock every 5 time units
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;
        
        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle T to set the flip-flop to "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0; // Ensure that T is toggled back

        // Finish simulation
        #30 $finish;
    end

endmodule

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // 10 time units period
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;

        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle the T flip-flop to the "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0; // Keep it stable to observe the state

        // Finish the simulation
        #20 $finish;
    end

    // Monitor outputs
    initial begin
        $monitor("At time %t: clk = %b, reset = %b, t = %b, q = %b", $time, clk, reset, t, q);
    end

endmodule

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // 10 time units period
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;

        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle the T flip-flop to "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0;

        // End simulation after some time
        #50 $finish;
    end

endmodule

    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // 10 time units period clock
    end

    initial begin
        // Initial conditions
        reset = 1;
        t = 0;
        
        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 0; // Release reset after 10 time units
        #10 t = 1;     // Set toggle input to 1 to toggle the state
        
        // Wait and observe the output
        #50 $stop;     // Stop simulation after 50 time units
    end

endmodule
Compilation check...

VERILOG CODE:
// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // 10 time units period
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;

        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle the T flip-flop to the "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0; // Keep it stable to observe the state

        // Finish the simulation
        #20 $finish;
    end

    // Monitor outputs
    initial begin
        $monitor("Time = %0t | clk = %b | reset = %b | t = %b | q = %b", $time, clk, reset, t, q);
    end

endmodule
Compilation check...

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // Toggle clock every 5 time units
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;

        #10 reset = 0;
        
        // Toggle to "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0; // Keep t low to maintain the state

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // 10 time units period
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;

        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle the T flip-flop to the "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0; // Keep it stable to observe the state

        // Finish the simulation
        #20 $finish;
    end

    // Monitor outputs
    initial begin
        $monitor("At time %t: clk = %b, reset = %b, t = %b, q = %b", $time, clk, reset, t, q);
    end

endmodule

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // 10 time units period
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;

        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle the T flip-flop to the "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0; // Keep it stable to observe the state

        // Finish the simulation
        #20 $finish;
    end

endmodule

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // Toggle clock every 5 time units
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;
        
        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle to "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0;

        // Finish simulation
        #50 $finish;
    end

endmodule

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // Toggle clock every 5 time units
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;
        
        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle T to set the flip-flop to "1"
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0; // Keep T low to maintain the state

        // Finish simulation
        #50 $finish;
    end

endmodule
Compilation check...

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // 10 time units period
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;

        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle the T flip-flop to "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0;

        // End simulation after some time
        #50 $finish;
    end

endmodule
Compilation check...
Verilog compilation failed, error:  14
